Two of the soups spilled. :/ I told the lady Gloria who was handling my order and asked if i would be able to get another soup she said yeah. She cleared the line of ppl. Her and another lady go to clean the spill. More ppl come in and she walks back behind the counter to take care of them. She starts taking the other lady. Now im having to interrupt her and ask her hey am i going to be able to get another soup. She said no sorry. < Review>
This place is near my work and I always see it when I pass by. I'm a big lover of ice cream and the ice cream cone statue outside caught my attention. It has a small parking lot and the store is tiny with only a few bar stools to sit down to enjoy the ice cream. The day I went with my coworker it was empty, so the server was able to dedicate time to us. He was friendly and answered all our questions. You can taste test a few samples and they have ice cream and bars.

There are many flavors available like cookies n cream, vanilla, chocolate chip, salted caramel, mango, strawberry, and hazelnut. You can order in a waffle cone or cups. The small cup is super tiny, and I love ice cream, so I thought it wasn't going to be enough. The medium size is a good portion and you can get 2 flavors. I ordered the chocolate chip and the gelato is smooth and creamy. It didn't taste bland or hard it was soft, and it melted perfectly with each bite. It's a must try if you're craving something sweet and it's a hot day. I will be back to try more flavors.<//Review>

< name>
Kristin Renk<//name>
<Date>1572016640377</Date><Rating>4</Rating><review>Pruneridge (or 'pruner' as my friends and I lovingly call it) is a cute little nine-hole golf course in Santa Clara right on Saratoga, a little bit off of San Thomas Expressway. I've been coming to hit balls and play golf at this course since I was a little girl. It has gone through some ownership changes, technology upgrades, landscaping, and price increases during its time, but it still remains one of the best places in the South Bay to play a quick nine or get some practice in.

The driving range is two-story (no driving allowed on the top level), and has an adjacent training area with state of the art computer programs that break down your swing, tell you how fast you are bringing the club through, etc. (you need to make an appointment for this service) and there is also a private driving range on a nice grass area for members on the other side of the training building. The chipping and putting areas are beautiful, well-manicured, and give you a good idea of how the greens play on the course.

The course itself can get a little crowded and backed up, as it's a great course for beginners. The holes are well landscaped and kept up nicely and it's a great place to spend an afternoon. The only thing you need to watch out for are balls coming over the net from the driving range on the right side of the ninth fairway! Otherwise, just enjoy yourself. And after your round, stop in to the little restaurant for a bite or the pro shop to upgrade your gear.

If you live in the South Bay and are a golfer, make sure to check out Pruneridge one of these days! You'll have a great time.< /review><pictures>None< /pictures>< response>

<user>105438298456977892227</user>< Review>
Wow these folks are great. I have been looking for a new Driver. After speaking with the staff I decided to get fit like a PGA Tour Pro. Best decision I have ever made with buying a new golf club. They had no allegiance with any manufacture. They let technology and the feedback from MY swing dictate the correct club for me. What a great experience. They only cared about getting me fit with the right Driver. After the whole thing was over I had to swing at it my home course. WOW!!! My slice is dead I am hitting it straight and can't wait to play with the boys this weekend. I hit 60 balls after work. 55 hit the target . That sounds like 90% better. It really felt like 100%. These guys know there stuff. I would recommend getting yourself or someone you know this process. They are going to be thrilled. To the staff at Pruneridge Golf Club, thanks for not selling me something off the rack. I have done that for 20 years. This is the real deal. You guys rock. Thanks Blair

< text>
Service at Chanel cosmetics is horrible!  The woman who "helped" me was peering down her nose at me.  I was painting one nail with a sample nail polish to see if the color was right.  This was Saturday April 7 at about 7pm. This tall Caucasian lady with light brownish hair piled on her head came by and looked at me as if I was stealing something or doing something wrong.  I told her I was deciding between 2 colors and she made an obvious suggestion (I suppose she thinks that me as 35 year old women doesn't the difference between spring and winter colors).  But her tone was condescending and she stood hovering over me pressuring me to make a decision as if she were afraid I was going to run off with the sample.  Under pressure I went and purchased one nail polish but will be returning it on Monday.  I mean buying Chanel cosmetics should be a pleasant experience, and every time I look at this bottle of nail polish I remember that rude sales woman.  I used to live in Los Angeles and before the recession purchased Chanel cosmetics all the time.  Since the cost of living is cheaper here in Fresno I was going to resume my Chanel cosmetic habit.  But I won't now.  If they can't hire people who will attend to me gracefully I will be spend my money on cosmetic brands that do.<//text>
